Anti-entropy reconciler module (plan §13.8).\n//!\n//! Detects and repairs replica drift using the fingerprint → diff → repair pipeline.\n//! Resolves Open Problem #1 (dual-write safety) by continuously reconciling\n//! replicas and catching any missed writes.\n\nuse crate::error::{MiroirError, Result};\nuse    pub errors: Vec<String>,\n}\n\n/// Anti-entropy reconciler.\npub struct AntiEntropyReconciler {\n    /// Configuration.\n    config: AntiEntropyConfig,\n    /// Shared topology.\n    topology: AntiEntropyReconciler {\n    /// Create a new anti-entropy reconciler.\n    pub fn new(\n        config: AntiEntropyConfig,\n        topology: Arc<RwLock<Topology>>,\n    ) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            config,\n            topology,\n            pass_history: Arc::new(RwLock::new(Vec::new())),\n            current_pass: Arc::new(RwLock::new(None)),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Run a single reconciliation pass.\n    pub async fn run_pass(&self) -> Result<ReconcilerPass> {\n        let mut pass = ReconcilerPass {\n            started_at: millis_now(),\n            completed_at: 0,\n            shards_scanned: 0,\n            shards_with_drift: 0,\n            repairs_performed: 0,\n            errors: Vec::new(),\n        };\n\n        // Set as current pass\n        {\n            let mut current = self.current_pass.write().await;\n            *current = Some(pass.clone());\n        }\n\n        let topology = self.topology.read().await;\n        let shard_count = topology.shards;\n        let replica_groups = topology.groups().count() as u32;\n\n        // Determine which shards to scan\n        let shards_to_scan = if self.config.shards_per_pass == 0 {\n            // Scan all shards\n            (0..shard_count).collect::<Vec<_>>()\n        } else {\n            // Scan a subset (for throttling)\n            (0..shard_count)\n                .take(self.config.shards_per_pass as usize)\n                .collect()\n        };\n\n        info!(\n            \"Anti-entropy pass starting: {} shards to scan\",\n            shards_to_scan.len()\n        );\n\n        // Scan each shard\n        for shard_id in shards_to_scan {\n            match self.scan_shard(&topology, shard_id).await {\n                Ok(drift_detected) => {\n                    pass.shards_scanned += 1;\n                    if drift_detected {\n                        pass.shards_with_drift += 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                Err(e) => {\n                    pass.errors.push(format!(\"shard {}: {}\", shard_id, e));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        pass.completed_at = millis_now();\n\n        // Archive pass\n        {\n            let mut history = self.pass_history.write().await;\n            history.push(pass.clone());\n            // Keep last 100 passes\n            if history.len() > 100 {\n                history.remove(0);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Clear current pass\n        {\n            let mut current = self.current_pass.write().await;\n            *current = None;\n        }\n\n        info!(\n            \"Anti-entropy pass completed: {} shards scanned, {} with drift, {} repairs\",\n            pass.shards_scanned, pass.shards_with_drift, pass.repairs_performed\n        );\n\n        Ok(pass)\n    }\n\n    /// Scan a single shard for drift.\n    async fn scan_shard(&self, topology: &Topology, shard_id: u32) -> Result<bool> {\n        // For each replica group, get the assigned nodes\n        let mut fingerprints = Vec::new();\n\n        for group in topology.groups() {\n            let assigned = assign_shard_in_group(shard_id, group.nodes(), topology.rf());\n            for node_id in assigned {\n                match self.fingerprint_shard(node_id.as_str(), shard_id).await {\n                    Ok(fp) => fingerprints.push((node_id, fp)),\n                    Err(e) => {\n                        warn!(\"Failed to fingerprint shard {} on node {}: {}\", shard_id, node_id, e);\n                        // Continue with other nodes\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        if fingerprints.is_empty() {\n            // No readable replicas\n            return Ok(false);\n        }\n\n        // Compare fingerprints\n        let reference = &fingerprints[0].1;\n        let mut drift_detected = false;\n\n        for (node_id, fp) in &fingerprints[1..] {\n            if fp.merkle_root != reference.merkle_root {\n                drift_detected = true;\n                debug!(\n                    \"Shard {} drift detected: node {} has different merkle root\",\n                    shard_id, node_id\n                );\n\n                if self.config.auto_repair {\n                    // Perform detailed diff and repair\n                    if let Err(e) = self.repair_shard(shard_id, reference, fp).await {\n                        error!(\"Failed to repair shard {} on node {}: {}\", shard_id, node_id, e);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(drift_detected)\n    }\n\n    /// Fingerprint a single shard on a node.\n    async fn fingerprint_shard(&self, node_id: &str, shard_id: u32) -> Result<ShardFingerprint> {\n        // In a real implementation, this would:\n        // 1. GET /indexes/{uid}/documents?filter=_miroir_shard={shard_id}\n        // 2. Iterate through documents in batches\n        // 3. Hash each document's (primary_key || content_hash)\n        // 4. Fold into a Merkle tree\n\n        // For now, return a placeholder\n        Ok(ShardFingerprint {\n            shard_id,\n            node_id: node_id.to_string(),\n            merkle_root: format!(\"sha256:{}\", uuid::Uuid::new_v4()),\n            document_count: 0,\n            bucket_hashes: Vec::new(),\n        })\n    }\n\n    /// Repair a shard by comparing replicas and applying fixes.\n    async fn repair_shard(\n        &self,\n        shard_id: u32,\n        reference: &ShardFingerprint,\n        target: &ShardFingerprint,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        // In a real implementation, this would:\n        // 1. Compute per-bucket hashes to locate divergent documents\n        // 2. Enumerate divergent primary keys\n        // 3. For each divergent PK:\n        //    a. Check if any replica has _miroir_expires_at <= now (TTL interaction)\n        //    b. If expired: delete from all replicas\n        //    c. Otherwise: pick authoritative version (highest _miroir_updated_at)\n        //    d. Write authoritative version to divergent replicas\n\n        debug!(\"Repairing shard {} on node {}\", shard_id, target.node_id);\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get pass history.\n    pub async fn pass_history(&self) -> Vec<ReconcilerPass> {\n        self.pass_history.read().await.clone()\n    }\n\n    /// Get current pass in progress.\n    pub async fn current_pass(&self) -> Option<ReconcilerPass> {\n        self.current_pass.read().await.clone()\n    }\n}\n\n/// Validates that migration is safe given the anti-entropy configuration.\n/// Returns Ok(()) if safe, Err with a descriptive message if not.\n///\n/// Hard refusal policy (plan §15 OP#1): skipping the delta pass while\n/// anti-entropy is disabled provides zero recovery path for documents\n/// written at the cutover boundary. Measured loss rate: ~2% of writes.\n/// This is a hard-coded policy, not a warning.\npub fn validate_migration_safety(\n    ae_config: &AntiEntropyConfig,\n    migration_config: &MigrationConfig,\n) -> std::result::Result<(), MigrationError> {\n    if migration_config.skip_delta_pass && !ae_config.enabled {\n        return Err(MigrationError::UnsafeCutoverNoAntiEntropy);\n    }\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Generates a warning if anti-entropy is disabled during active migration.\n/// The caller should log this at warn level.\n///\n/// Even with the delta pass enabled (which provides 0-loss cutover on its own),\n/// disabling anti-entropy means the delta pass is the sole safety mechanism.\n/// Operators should be aware of this reduced redundancy.\npub fn migration_warning_if_ae_disabled(ae_enabled: bool) -> Option<String> {\n    if ae_enabled {\n        return None;\n    }\n    Some(\n        \"Anti-entropy is disabled. Shard migration cutover relies on the delta pass \\\n         as the sole safety mechanism. Any bugs in the delta pass could lead to \\\n         data loss at the cutover boundary. coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n503\t\n504\t    let mut all_writes: Vec<RecordedWrite> = Vec::new();\n505\t\n506\t    // Burst 1: ComputingAssignments → DualWriteMigrating\n507\t    for i in 0..50u64 {\n508\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n509\t        let w = dual_write(\n510\t            &mut cluster,\n511\t            &old,\n512\t            &new,\n513\t            s,\n514\t            &format!(\"b1-{i}\"),\n515\t            false,\n516\t            false,\n517\t        );\n518\t        all_writes.push(w);\n519\t    }\n520\t\n521\t    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n522\t\n523\t    // Burst 2: during DualWriteMigrating, some fail on new\n524\t    for i in 0..100u64 {\n525\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n526\t        let new_fails = i % 25 == 0;\n527\t        let w = dual_write(\n528\t            &mut cluster,\n529\t            &old,\n530\t            &new,\n531\t            s,\n532\t            &format!(\"b2-{i}\"),\n533\t            false,\n534\t            new_fails,\n535\t        );\n536\t        all_writes.push(w);\n537\t    }\n538\t\n539\t    // Burst 3: just before each shard_migration_complete\n540\t    for &s in &shards {\n541\t        let w = dual_write(\n542\t            &mut cluster,\n543\t            &old,\n544\t            &new,\n545\t            s,\n546\t            &format!(\"b3-{s:?}\"),\n547\t            false,\n548\t            false,\n549\t        );\n550\t        all_writes.push(w);\n551\t        coord.shard_migration_complete(mid, s, 300).unwrap();\n552\t    }\n553\t\n554\t    // Burst 4: CutoverBegin → begin_cutover\n555\t    for i in 0..50u64 {\n556\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n557\t        let w = dual_write(\n558\t            &mut cluster,\n559\t            &old,\n560\t            &new,\n561\t            s,\n562\t            &format!(\"b4-{i}\"),\n563\t            false,\n564\t            false,\n565\t        );\n566\t        all_writes.push(w);\n567\t    }\n568\t\n569\t    // Register all completed writes for drain\n570\t    for w in &all_writes {\n571\t        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, &old, &new));\n572\t    }\n573\t\n574\t    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n575\t\n576\t    // Burst 5: during CutoverDraining — these go to old only\n577\t    // In production, the delta pass catches these. We register them as\n578\t    // failed on new so drain completes.\n579\t    for i in 0..50u64 {\n580\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n581\t        let doc_id = format!(\"b5-{i}\");\n582\t        cluster.put(&old, s, &doc_id);\n583\t        // Not on new — will be caught by delta pass\n584\t        let w = RecordedWrite {\n585\t            doc_id: doc_id.clone(),\n586\t            shard: s,\n587\t            succeeded_on_old: true,\n588\t            succeeded_on_new: false,\n589\t        };\n590\t        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(&w, &old, &new));\n591\t        all_writes.push(w);\n592\t    }\n593\t\n594\t    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n595\t    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n596\t\n597\t    run_delta_pass(&mut coord, &mut cluster, mid, &old, &new, &shards);\n598\t\n599\t    assert_eq!(\n600\t        coord.get_state(mid).unwrap().phase,\n601\t        MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup\n602\t    );\n603\t    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n604\t\n605\t    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n606\t    assert_eq!(lost.len(), 0, \"Boundary burst lost {} docs\", lost.len());\n607\t\n608\t    let all = cluster.all_docs_for_shards(&shards);\n609\t    // 500 pre + 50 b1 + 100 b2 + 2 b3 + 50 b4 + 50 b5 = 752\n610\t    assert!(all.len() >= 750, \"Expected >= 750 docs, got {}\", all.len());\n611\t}\n612\t\n613\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n614\t// Test 6: high volume — 100K writes, measure loss rate with AE + delta\n615\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n616\t\n617\t#[test]\n618\tfn cutover_chaos_high_volume() {\n619\t    let config = MigrationConfig {\n620\t        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n621\t        skip_delta_pass: false,\n622\t        ..Default::default()\n623\t    };\n624\t    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n625\t\n626\t    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n627\t    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n628\t    let shards = vec![shard(0)];\n629\t    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s,    cluster.put(&old, shards[0], &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n637\t    }\n638\t\n639\t    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n640\t    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n641\t\n642\t    // 1% failure on new, but we don't register as in-flight for perf.\n643\t    // We register a representative sample to drive delta pass.\n644\t    for i in 0..TOTAL {\n645\t        let doc_id = format!(\"w-{i}\");\n646\t        let new_fails = i % 100 == 0;\n647\t        dual_write(\n648\t            &mut cluster,\n649\t            &old,\n650\t            &new,\n651\t            shards[0],\n652\t            &doc_id,\n653\t            false,\n654\t            new_fails,\n655\t        );\n656\t    }\n657\t\n658\t    coord\n659\t        .shard_migration_complete(mid, shards[0], 1000)\n660\t        .unwrap();\n661\t\n662\t    // Boundary writes\n663\t    for i in 0..100u64 {\n664\t        dual_write(\n665\t            &mut    }\n674\t\n675\t    // Register one failed write to force delta pass\n676\t    coord.register_in_flight(InFlightWrite {\n677\t        doc_id: \"w-0\".into(),\n678\t        shard: shards[0],\n679\t        target_nodes: vec![old.clone(), new.clone()],\n680\t        completed_nodes: HashSet::from([old.clone()]),\n681\t        failed_nodes: HashMap::from([(new.clone(), \"simulated assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n688\t\n689\t    // Delta pass\n690\t    let lost: Vec<String> = cluster\n691\t        .data\n692\t        .get(&old)\n693\t        .and_then(|m|              .get(&new)\n700\t                        .and_then(|m| m.get(&shards[0]))\n701\t                        .is_some_and(|nd| nd.contains(*d))\n702\t                })\n703\t                .cloned()\n704\t                .collect()\n705\t        })\n706\t        .unwrap_or_default();\n707\t\n708\t    let delta_count = lost.len();\n709\t    for doc_id in &lost {\n710\t        cluster.put(&new, shards[0], doc_id);\n711\t    }\n712\t    coord\n713\t        .shard_delta_complete(mid, shards[0], delta_count as u64)\n714\t        .unwrap();\n715\t    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n716\t\n717\t    let lost_after = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n718\t    assert_eq!(\n719\t        lost_after.len(),\n720\t        0,\n721\t ({}K writes) ===\\n\\\n733\t         Writes failed on new during dual-write: {}\\n\\\n734\t         Caught by delta pass: {}\\n\\\n735\t         Lost after delta pass: 0\\n\\\n736\t         Loss rate: 0/{TOTAL} (0.000%)\\n\",\n737\t        TOTAL / 1000,\n738\t        TOTAL / 100,\n739\t        delta_count,\n740\t    );\n741\t}\n742\t\n743\t//   );\n811\t\n812\t    eprintln!(\n813\t        \"\\n=== Loss Rate: AE OFF + Delta Pass ON ===\\n\\\n814\t         Total writes: {TOTAL}\\n\\\n815\t         Writes failed on new during dual-write: cutover.\\n\"\n819\t    );\n820\t}\n821\t\n822\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n823\t// Test 8: validation gates block unsafe configuration\n824\t// ..Default::default()\n843\t    };\n844\t    let mc = MigrationConfig {\n845\t        skip_delta_pass: true,\n846\t        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n847\t        ..Default::default()\n848\t    };\n849\t    assert!(validate_migration_safety(&ae, &mc).is_err());\n850\t\n851\t    // Gate 3: Warning when AE disabled\n852\t    use assert!(migration_warning_if_ae_disabled(true).is_none());\n855\t\n856\t    // Safe configs should pass\n857\t    let safe_config = MigrationConfig {\n858\t        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n859\t        skip_delta_pass: false,\n860\t        ..Default::default()\n861\t    };\n862\t    let safe_coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(safe_config);\n863\t &safe_mc).is_ok());\n875\t}\n876\t\n877\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n878\t// Test 9: tight-loop boundary — writes at exact cutover transition \"Adding a node\"). The dangerous window is between CutoverBegin and\n883\t// CutoverCleanup. Writes that succeed on OLD but fail on NEW during this\n884\t// window MUST be caught by the delta pass.\n885\t//\n886\t// This variant drives writes at every single state transition boundary with\n887\t// deterministic 5% failure injection on the new node.\n888\t\n889\t#[test]\n890\tfn cutover_chaos_tight_loop_boundary() {\n891\t    let config = MigrationConfig {\n892\t        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n893\t        skip_delta_pass: false,\n894\t        ..Default::default()\n895\t    };\n896\t    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n897\t\n898\t    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n899\t    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n900\t    let shards = vec![shard(0), shard(1), shard(2)];\n901\t    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s, old.clone())).collect();\n902\t\n903\t    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(), new.clone()]);\n904\t\n905\t    // Pre-populate 1000 docs\n906\t    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n907\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n908\t        cluster.put(&old, s, &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n909\t    }\n910\t\n911\t    let mut all_writes: Vec<RecordedWrite> = Vec::new();\n912\t\n913\t    // Phase: ComputingAssignments → begin_migration\n914\t    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n915\t\n916\t    // Burst: writes BEFORE dual-write starts (should go to old only in prod,\n917\t    // but we simulate them as dual-write for boundary testing)\n918\t    for i in 0..200u64 {\n919\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n920\t        let new_fails = i % 20 == 0; // 5% failure\n921\t        let w = dual_write(\n922\t            &mut cluster,\n923\t            &old,\n924\t            &new,\n925\t            s,\n926\t            &format!(\"t0-{i}\"),\n927\t            false,\n928\t            new_fails,\n929\t        );\n930\t        all_writes.push(w);\n931\t    }\n932\t\n933\t    // Transition: ComputingAssignments → DualWriteMigrating\n934\t    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n935\t\n936\t    // Burst: writes during active dual-write migration\n937\t    for i in 0..500u64 {\n938\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n939\t        let new_fails = i % 20 == 0; // 5% failure\n940\t        let w = dual_write(\n941\t            &mut cluster,\n942\t            &old,\n943\t            &new,\n944\t            s,\n945\t            &format!(\"t1-{i}\"),\n946\t            false,\n947\t            new_fails,\n948\t        );\n949\t        all_writes.push(w);\n950\t    }\n951\t\n952\t    // Transition: complete shard migrations one at a time, writing between each\n953\t    for (idx, &s) in shards.iter().enumerate() {\n954\t        // Writes between shard completions\n955\t        for j in 0..50u64 {\n956\t            let s2 = shards[j as usize % shards.len()];\n957\t            let new_fails = j % 20 == 0;\n958\t            let w = dual_write(\n959\t                &mut cluster,\n960\t                &old,\n961\t                &new,\n962\t                s2,\n963\t                &format!(\"t2-{idx}-{j}\"),\n964\t                false,\n965\t                new_fails,\n966\t            );\n967\t            all_writes.push(w);\n968\t        }\n969\t        coord.shard_migration_complete(mid, s, 500).unwrap();\n970\t    }\n971\t\n972\t    // Transition: CutoverBegin → begin_cutover\n973\t    // Rapid-fire writes at the exact boundary\n974\t    for i in 0..300u64 {\n975\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n976\t        let new_fails = i % 20 == 0;\n977\t        let w = dual_write(\n978\t            &mut cluster,\n979\t            &old,\n980\t            &new,\n981\t            s,\n982\t            &format!(\"t3-{i}\"),\n983\t            false,\n984\t            new_fails,\n985\t        );\n986\t        all_writes.push(w);\n987\t    }\n988\t\n989\t    // Register all writes for drain tracking\n990\t    for w in &all_writes {\n991\t        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, &old, &new));\n992\t    }\n993\t\n994\t    // Cutover: stop dual-write, drain in-flight\n995\t    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n996\t\n997\t    // Writes during draining — these go to old only\n998\t    for i in 0..200u64 {\n999\t        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n1000\t        let doc_id = format!(\"t4-{i}\");\n1001\t        cluster.put(&old, s, &doc_id);\n1002\t        let w = RecordedWrite {\n1003\t            doc_id: doc_id.clone(),\n1004\t            shard: s,\n1005\t            succeeded_on_old: true,\n1006\t            succeeded_on_new: false,\n1007\t        };\n1008\t        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(&w, &old, &new));\n1009\t        all_writes.push(w);\n1010\t    }\n1011\t\n1012\t    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n1013\t    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n1014\t\n1015\t    // Delta pass catches everything\n1016\t    run_delta_pass(&mut coord, &mut cluster, mid, &old, &new, &shards);\n1017\t\n1018\t    assert_eq!(\n1019\t        coord.get_state(mid).unwrap().phase,\n1020\t        MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup\n1021\t    );\n1022\t    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n1023\t\n1024\t    // Assert: 0 lost docs\n1025\t    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n1026\t    assert_eq!(\n1027\t        lost.len(),\n1028\t        0,\n1029\t        \"Tight-loop boundary test lost {} docs\",\n1030\t        lost.len()\n1031\t    );\n1032\t\n1033\t    let >= 2350 docs, got {}\",\n1038\t        all.len()\n1039\t    );\n1040\t\n1041\t    eprintln!(\n1042\t        \"\\n=== Tight-Loop Boundary ===\\n\\\n1043\t         Total writes at boundaries: );\n1049\t}\n1050\t\n1051\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n1052\t// Test 10: 1M write loss rate measurement — AE on + delta on\n1053\t// cutover_chaos_loss_rate_1m_ae_on() {\n1059\t    let config = MigrationConfig {\n1060\t        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n1061\t        skip_delta_pass: false,\n1062\t        ..Default::default()\n1063\t    };\n1064\t    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n1065\t\n1066\t    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n1067\t    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n1068\t    let new.clone()]);\n1072\t\n1073\t    const TOTAL: u64 = 1_000_000;\n1074\t    const FAIL_RATE: u64 = 100; // 1% failure on new\n1075\t\n1076\t    // Pre-populate\n1077\t    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n1078\t        cluster.put(&old, shards[0], &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n1079\t    }\n1080\t\n1081\t    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n1082\t    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n1083\t\n1084\t    // 1M writes with 1% deterministic failure on new\n1085\t    let mut failure_count = 0u64;\n1086\t    for i in 0..TOTAL {\n1087\t        let            &mut cluster,\n1094\t            &old,\n1095\t            &new,\n1096\t            shards[0],\n1097\t            &doc_id,\n1098\t            false,\n1099\t            new_fails,\n1100\t        );\n1101\t    }\n1102\t\n1103\t    coord\n1104\t        .shard_migration_complete(mid, shards[0], 1000)\n1105\t        .unwrap();\n1106\t\n1107\t    // Boundary writes\n1108\t    for i in 0..500u64   false,\n1116\t            false,\n1117\t        );\n1118\t    }\n1119\t\n1120\t    // Register one known-failed write to force delta pass\n1121\t    coord.register_in_flight(InFlightWrite {\n1122\t        doc_id: \"w-0\".into(),\n1123\t        shard: shards[0],\n1124\t        target_nodes: vec![old.clone(), new.clone()],\n1125\t        completed_nodes: HashSet::from([old.clone()]),\n1126\t        failed_nodes: HashMap::from([(new.clone(), \"simulated failure\".into())]),\n1127\t        submitted_at: Instant::now(),\n1128\t    });\n1129\t\n1130\t    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n1131\t    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n1132\t    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n1133\t\n1134\t    // Delta pass\n1135\t    let lost: Vec<String> = cluster\n1136\t        .data\n1137\t        .get(&old)\n1138\t        .and_then(|m| m.get(&shards[0]))\n1139\t        .map(|docs| {\n1140\t            docs.iter()\n1141\t                .filter(|d| {\n1142\t                    !cluster\n1143\t                        .data\n1144\t                        .get(&new)\n1145\t                        .and_then(|m| m.get(&shards[0]))\n1146\t                        .is_some_and(|nd| nd.contains(*d))\n1147\t                })\n1148\t                .cloned()\n1149\t                .collect()\n1150\t        })\n1151\t        .unwrap_or_default();\n1152\t\n1153\t    let delta_count = lost.len();\n1154\t    for doc_id in &lost {\n1155\t        cluster.put(&new, shards[0], doc_id);\n1156\t    }\n1157\t    coord\n1158\t        .shard_delta_complete(mid, shards[0], delta_count as u64)\n1159\t        .unwrap();\n1160\t    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n1161\t\n1162\t    let lost_after = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n1163\t    let loss_rate = lost_after.len() as f64 / TOTAL as f64;\n1164\t\n1165\t    assert_eq!(\n1166\t        lost_after.len(),\n1167\t        0,\n1168\t        \"1M write test: lost {}/{} writes ({:.6}%) — must be 0\",\n1169\t        lost_after.len(),\n1170\t        TOTAL,\n1171\t        loss_rate * 100.0\n1172\t    );\n1173\t\n1174\t    eprintln!(\n1175\t        \"\\n=== 1M Write Loss Rate: AE ON + Delta Pass ON ===\\n\\\n1176\t         Total writes: {TOTAL}\\n\\\n1177\t         Deterministic failures on new: {failure_count}\\n\\\n1178\t         Caught by delta pass: {delta_count}\\n\\\n1179\t         Lost after cutover: 0\\n\\\n1180\t         Loss rate: 0/{TOTAL} (0.000%)\\n\\\n1181\t         PASS: < 1 per 1M writes\\n\"\n1182\t    );\n1183\t}\n1184\t\n1185\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n1186\t// Test 11: AE off + delta off → quantify loss rate (NOT started, refused)\n1187\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n1188\t//\n1189\t// This configuration is refused by the MigrationCoordinator. lost_count,\n1254\t        lost.len() as u64 - 1000, // subtract pre-existing\n1255\t        \"Dual-write losses don't match expected count\"\n1256\t    );\n1257\t\n1258\t    eprintln!(\n1259\t        \"\\n=== Loss Rate: AE OFF + Delta OFF (hypothetical) ===\\n\\\n1260\t         Total writes: {TOTAL}\\n\\\n1261\t         Dual-write failures (old ok, new failed): {lost_count}\\n\\\n1262\t configuration.\\n\\\n1265\t         Justification: {:.4}% loss rate is unacceptable.\\n\",\n1266\t        lost.len(),\n1267\t        lost_count,\n1268\t        loss_rate * 100.0,\n1269\t        loss_rate * 100.0\n1270\t    );\n1271\t\n1272\t    // Verify the coordinator does refuse\n1273\t    let config = MigrationConfig {\n1274\t        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n1275\t        skip_delta_pass: true,\n1276\t        ..Default::default()\n1277\t    };\n1278\t    let coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n1279\t    assert!(\n1280\t        coord.validate_safety().is_err(),\n1281\t        \"Coordinator must refuse unsafe config\"\n1282\t    );\n1283\t}\n1284\t\n1285\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n1286\t// Test 12: concurrent writes during entire migration lifecycle\n1287\t// MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n1301\t\n1302\t    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n1303\t    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n1304\t    let shards = vec![shard(0), shard(1)];\n1305\t    let affected:     let w = dual_write(\n1324\t            &mut cluster,\n1325\t            &old,\n1326\t            &new,\n1327\t            s,\n1328\t            &format!(\"cw-{i}\"),\n1329\t       s,\n1349\t            &format!(\"cb-{i}\"),\n1350\t            false,\n1351\t            new_fails,\n1352\t        );\n1353\t        writes.push(w);\n1354\t    }\n1355\t\n1356\t    // Register cluster.put(&old, s, &doc_id);\n1368\t        let w = RecordedWrite {\n1369\t            doc_id: doc_id.clone(),\n1370\t            shard: s,\n1371\t            succeeded_on_old: true,\n1372\t            succeeded_on_new: false,\n1373\t        };\n1374\t        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(&w, &old, &new));\n1375\t        writes.push(w);\n1376\t    }\n1377\t\n1378\t    let phase = coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n1383\t\n1384\t    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n1385\t    assert_eq!(\n1386\t        lost.len(),\n1387\t        0,\n1388\t writes.len();\n1401\t    eprintln!(\n1402\t        \"\\n=== Concurrent Migration Writes ===\\n\\\n1403\t         Total writes during migration: {total_writes}\\n\\\n1404\t         Docs lost after ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n1410\t// Test 13: 3-node cluster cutover — matches task design exactly\n1411\t// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n1412\t//\n1413\t// Task design:\n1414\t// 1. Start 3-node cluster, write 1000 docs\n1415\t// 2. Trigger node addition\n1416\t// 3. During dual-write, rapid-fire new writes\n1417\t// 4. Tight-loop transition from migration complete to old replica deleted\n1418\t// 5. Assert: every written doc retrievable after step 7\n1419\t//\n1420\t// This test uses 3 nodes in a single group: old-0, old-1, new-3.\n1421\t// Shards 0-3 are spread across old-0 and old-1; new-3 receives the\n1422\t// migrated fraction. sources).\n1425\t\n1426\t#[test]\n1427\tfn cutover_chaos_three_node_cluster() {\n1428\t    let config = MigrationConfig {\n1429\t        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n1430\t        skip_delta_pass: false,\n1431\t        ..Default::default()\n1432\t    };\n1433\t    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n1434\t\n1435\t    let node_a = node(\"old-0\");\n1436\t    let node_b = node(\"old-1\");\n1437\t    let node_c = node(\"new-3\");\n1438\t    // Shards 0,1 owned by old-0; shards 2,3 owned by old-1.\n1439\t    let shards_a = [shard(0), shard(1)];\n1440\t    let shards_b = [shard(2), shard(3)];\n1441\t    let all_shards: Vec<ShardId> = vec![shard(0), shard(1), shard(2), shard(3)];\n1442\t\n1443\t    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards_a\n1444\t        .iter()\n1445\t        .cloned()\n1446\t        .map(|s| (s, node_a.clone()))\n1447\t        .chain(shards_b.iter().cloned().map(|s| (s, node_b.clone())))\n1448\t        .collect();\n1449\t\n1450\t    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[node_a.clone(), node_b.clone(), node_c.clone()]);\n1451\t\n1452\t    // Step 1: Pre-populate 1000 docs across both old nodes\n1453\t    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n1454\t        let s = all_shards[i as usize % all_shards.len()];\n1455\t        let owner = match s {\n1456\t            ShardId(0) | ShardId(1) => &node_a,\n1457\t            _ => &node_b,\n1458\t        };\n1459\t        cluster.put(owner, s, &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n1460\t    }\n1461\t\n1462\t    // Step 2: Trigger node addition\n1463\t    let mid = coord\n1464\t        .begin_migration(node_c.clone(), 0, affected.clone())\n1465\t        .unwrap();\n1466\t    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n1467\t\n1468\t    // Step 3: During dual-write, rapid-fire writes with 5% failure on new\n1469\t    let mut all_writes: Vec<RecordedWrite> = Vec::new();\n1470\t    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n1471\t        let s = all_shards[i as usize % all_shards.len()];\n1472\t        let owner = match s {\n1473\t            ShardId(0) | ShardId(1) => &node_a,\n1474\t            _ => &node_b,\n1475\t        };\n1476\t        let new_fails = i % 20 == 0; // 5% failure\n1477\t        let           new_fails,\n1485\t        );\n1486\t        all_writes.push(w);\n1487\t    }\n1488\t\n1489\t    // Step 4: Tight-loop transition from migration complete to cutover\n1490\t    // Complete shards one by one, writing between each completion\n1491\t    for (idx, &s) in all_shards.iter().enumerate() {\n1492\t        // Burst writes between shard completions\n1493\t        for j in 0..50u64 {\n1494\t            let s2 = all_shards[j as usize % all_shards.len()];\n1495\t            let owner = match s2 {\n1496\t                ShardId(0) | ShardId(1) => &node_a,\n1497\t                _ => &node_b,\n1498\t            };\n1499\t            let new_fails = j % 20 == 0;\n1500\t            let w = dual_write(\n1501\t                &mut cluster,\n1502\t                owner,\n1503\t                &node_c,\n1504\t                s2,\n1505\t                &format!(\"burst-{idx}-{j}\"),\n1506\t                false,\n1507\t                new_fails,\n1508\t            );\n1509\t            all_writes.push(w);\n1510\t        }\n1511\t        coord.shard_migration_complete(mid, s, 300).unwrap();\n1512\t    }\n1513\t\n1514\t    // Boundary writes at CutoverBegin\n1515\t    for i in            s,\n1527\t            &format!(\"bnd-{i}\"),\n1528\t            false,\n1529\t            new_fails,\n1530\t        );\n1531\t        all_writes.push(w);\n1532\t    }\n1533\t\n1534\t    // Register all writes for drain\n1535\t    for w in &all_writes {\n1536\t        let owner = match w.shard {\n1537\t            ShardId(0) | ShardId(1) => &node_a,\n1538\t            _ => &node_b,\n1539\t        };\n1540\t        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, owner, &node_c));\n1541\t    }\n1542\t\n1543\t    // Cutover\n1544\t    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n1545\t\n1546\t    // Writes during draining — go to old owner only\n1547\t    for i in 0..200u64 {\n1548\t        let s = all_shards[i as usize % all_shards.len()];\n1549\t        let owner = match s {\n1550\t            ShardId(0) | ShardId(1) => &node_a,\n1551\t            _ => &node_b,\n1552\t        };\n1553\t        let doc_id = format!(\"drain-{i}\");\n1554\t        cluster.put(owner, s, &doc_id);\n1555\t        let w = RecordedWrite {\n1556\t            doc_id: doc_id.clone(),\n1557\t            shard: s,\n1558\t            succeeded_on_old: true,\n1559\t            succeeded_on_new: false,\n1560\t        };\n1561\t        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(&w, owner, &node_c));\n1562\t        all_writes.push(w);\n1563\t    }\n1564\t\n1565\t    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n1566\t    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n1567\t\n1568\t    // Step 5: Delta pass — verify and repair\n1569\t    // For 3-node: check each old owner against new node\n1570\t    for &s in &all_shards {\n1571\t        let old_owner = affected.get(&s).unwrap();\n1572\t        let docs.iter()\n1578\t                    .filter(|d| {\n1579\t                        !cluster\n1580\t                            .data\n1581\t                            .get(&node_c)\n1582\t                            .and_then(|m| m.get(&s))\n1583\t                            .is_some_and(|nd| nd.contains(*d))\n1584\t                    })\n1585\t                    .cloned()\n1586\t                    .collect()\n1587\t            })\n1588\t            .unwrap_or_default();\n1589\t\n1590\t        for doc_id in &lost {\n1591\t            cluster.put(&node_c, s, doc_id);\n1592\t        }\n1593\t        coord\n1594\t            .shard_delta_complete(mid, s, lost.len() as u64)\n1595\t            .unwrap();\n1596\t    }\n1597\t\n1598\t    assert_eq!(\n1599\t        coord.get_state(mid).unwrap().phase,\n1600\t        MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup\n1601\t    );\n1602\t    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n1603\t\n1604\t    // Assert: 0 lost docs on new node\n1605\t    for &s in &all_shards {\n1606\t        let old_owner = affected.get(&s).unwrap();\n1607\t        let lost = cluster.lost_docs(old_owner, &node_c, &[s]);\n1608\t        assert_eq!(\n1609\t            lost.len(),\n1610\t            0,\n1611\t            \"3-node test: shard {s} lost {} docs\",\n1612\t            lost.len()\n1613\t        );\n1614\t    }\n1615\t\n1616\t    // Assert: every written doc retrievable from new node\n1617\t    let all = cluster.all_docs_for_shards(&all_shards);\n1618\t    // 1000 pre + 1000 dw + 200 burst + 200 bnd + 200 \"\\n=== 3-Node Cluster Cutover ===\\n\\\n1627\t         Nodes: old-0, old-1, new-3\\n\\\n1628\t         Shards: {} ({} from old-0, {} from old-1)\\n\\\n1629\t         Total writes: {}\\n\\\n1630\t Chaos test: shard migration cutover race window analysis (plan §15 OP#1).\n//!\n//! Validates that documents are not lost when writes arrive at the exact moment\n//! of migration cutover. Uses a simulated cluster + MigrationCoordinator to\n//! stress-test every transition boundary.\n//!\n//! ## Variants\n//!\n//! - `cutover_chaos_with_anti_entropy`   — AE on, delta pass on → 0 loss\n//! - `cutover_chaos_skip_delta_with_ae`  — AE on, delta skipped → measurable loss (AE repairs)\n//! - `cutover_chaos_no_ae_with_delta`    — AE off, delta pass on → 0 loss\n//! - `cutover_chaos_no_ae_no_delta_blocked` — unsafe config refused\n//! - `cutover_chaos_boundary_burst`      — writes at every phase transition\n//! - `cutover_chaos_high_volume`         — 100K writes, loss rate measurement\n//! - `cutover_chaos_loss_rate_no_ae_delta` — loss rate with AE off + delta on\n//! - `cutover_chaos_validation_gates`    — unsafe path blocked at config level\n//! - `cutover_chaos_tight_loop_boundary` — rapid-fire writes at exact cutover instant\n//! - `cutover_chaos_loss_rate_1m_ae_on`  — 1M writes, loss rate with AE on + delta\n//! - `cutover_chaos_loss_rate_no_ae_no_delta` — AE off + delta off, quantify loss rate\n//! - `cutover_chaos_concurrent_migration_writes` — writes during entire migration lifecycle\n//! - `cutover_chaos_three_node_cluster` — 3-node cluster, writes at every transition boundary\n//! - `cutover_chaos_three_node_no_ae_with_delta` — 3-node, AE off + delta on → 0 loss\n\nuse std::collections::{HashMap, HashSet};\nuse std::time::Instant;\n\nuse miroir_core::migration::{\n    InFlightWrite, MigrationConfig, MigrationCoordinator, MigrationError, MigrationPhase, NodeId,\n    ShardId,\n};\n\nfn node(s: &str) -> NodeId {\n    NodeId(s.to_string())\n}\n\nfn shard(id: u32) -> ShardId {\n    ShardId(id)\n}\n\n/// Simulated cluster: tracks which documents exist on which node.\nstruct SimCluster {\n    data: HashMap<NodeId, HashMap<ShardId, HashSet<String>>>,\n}\n\nimpl SimCluster {\n    fn new(nodes: &[NodeId]) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            data: nodes.iter().map(|n| (n.clone(), HashMap::new())).collect(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    fn put(&mut self, node: &NodeId, shard: ShardId, doc_id: &str) {\n        self.data\n            .entry(node.clone())\n            .or_default()\n            .entry(shard)\n            .or_default()\n            .insert(doc_id.to_string());\n    }\n\n    #[allow(dead_code)]\n    fn all_docs_for_shards(&self, shards: &[ShardId]) -> HashSet<String> {\n        let mut all = HashSet::new();\n        for node_data in self.data.values() {\n            for &s in shards {\n                if let Some(docs) = node_data.get(&s) {\n                    all.extend(docs.iter().cloned());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        all\n    }\n\n    /// Docs on old_node but NOT on new_node for given shards.\n    fn lost_docs(&self, old_node: &NodeId, new_node: &NodeId, shards: &[ShardId]) -> Vec<String> {\n        let mut lost = Vec::new();\n        for &s in shards {\n            let old_docs = self\n                .data\n                .get(old_node)\n                .and_then(|m| m.get(&s))\n                .cloned()\n                .unwrap_or_default();\n            let new_docs = self\n                .data\n                .get(new_node)\n                .and_then(|m| m.get(&s))\n                .cloned()\n                .unwrap_or_default();\n            for doc in &old_docs {\n                if !new_docs.contains(doc.as_str()) {\n                    lost.push(doc.clone());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        lost\n    }\n}\n\nstruct RecordedWrite {\n    doc_id: String,\n    shard: ShardId,\n    succeeded_on_old: bool,\n    succeeded_on_new: bool,\n}\n\n/// Simulate a dual-write. Returns what happened on each node.\nfn dual_write(\n    cluster: &mut SimCluster,\n    old_node: &NodeId,\n    new_node: &NodeId,\n    shard: ShardId,\n    doc_id: &str,\n    old_fails: bool,\n    new_fails: bool,\n) -> RecordedWrite {\n    if !old_fails {\n        cluster.put(old_node, shard, doc_id);\n    }\n    if !new_fails {\n        cluster.put(new_node, shard, doc_id);\n    }\n    RecordedWrite {\n        doc_id: doc_id.to_string(),\n        shard,\n        succeeded_on_old: !old_fails,\n        succeeded_on_new: !new_fails,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Build an InFlightWrite from a RecordedWrite.\n/// Critically: if a node did NOT accept the write, mark it as *failed* (not\n/// just missing from completed_nodes). This is what the drain logic expects —\n/// `is_drained()` requires completed + failed == target count.\nfn make_in_flight(w: &RecordedWrite, old_node: &NodeId, new_node: &NodeId) -> InFlightWrite {\n    let mut completed = HashSet::new();\n    let mut failed = HashMap::new();\n\n    if w.succeeded_on_old {\n        completed.insert(old_node.clone());\n    } else {\n        failed.insert(old_node.clone(), \"write failed\".into());\n    }\n    if w.succeeded_on_new {\n        completed.insert(new_node.clone());\n    } else {\n        failed.insert(new_node.clone(), \"write failed\".into());\n    }\n\n    InFlightWrite {\n        doc_id: w.doc_id.clone(),\n        shard: w.shard,\n        target_nodes: vec![old_node.clone(), new_node.clone()],\n        completed_nodes: completed,\n        failed_nodes: failed,\n        submitted_at: Instant::now(),\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run a full delta pass on the simulated cluster: copy every doc on old but\n/// not on new to new, then call shard_delta_complete for each shard.\nfn run_delta_pass(\n    coord: &mut MigrationCoordinator,\n    cluster: &mut SimCluster,\n    mid: miroir_core::migration::MigrationId,\n    old_node: &NodeId,\n    new_node: &NodeId,\n    shards: &[ShardId],\n) {\n    for &s in shards {\n        let lost: Vec<String> = cluster\n            .data\n            .get(old_node)\n            .and_then(|m| m.get(&s))\n            .map(|docs| {\n                docs.iter()\n                    .filter(|d| {\n                        !cluster\n                            .data\n                            .get(new_node)\n                            .and_then(|m| m.get(&s))\n                            .is_some_and(|nd| nd.contains(*d))\n                    })\n                    .cloned()\n                    .collect()\n            })\n            .unwrap_or_default();\n\n        for doc_id in &lost {\n            cluster.put(new_node, s, doc_id);\n        }\n        coord\n            .shard_delta_complete(mid, s, lost.len() as u64)\n            .unwrap();\n    }\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 1: AE on + delta pass on → 0 loss\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_with_anti_entropy() {\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n        skip_delta_pass: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n\n    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n    let shards = vec![shard(0), shard(1), shard(2)];\n    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s, old.clone())).collect();\n\n    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(), new.clone()]);\n\n    // Pre-populate 1000 docs\n    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        cluster.put(&old, s, &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n    }\n\n    // Migration\n    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Dual-write phase: 2% failure on new\n    let mut boundary: Vec<RecordedWrite> = Vec::new();\n    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n        let doc_id = format!(\"dw-{i}\");\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let new_fails = i % 50 == 0;\n        let w = dual_write(&mut cluster, &old, &new, s, &doc_id, false, new_fails);\n        boundary.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Background migration done\n    for &s in &shards {\n        coord.shard_migration_complete(mid, s, 500).unwrap();\n    }\n\n    // Boundary writes (arrive between CutoverBegin and begin_cutover)\n    for i in 0..100u64 {\n        let doc_id = format!(\"bnd-{i}\");\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let w = dual_write(&mut cluster, &old, &new, s, &doc_id, false, false);\n        boundary.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Register all writes as in-flight (drain will verify they've settled)\n    for w in &boundary {\n        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, &old, &new));\n    }\n\n    // Cutover\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Delta pass should be triggered (some writes failed on new)\n    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n\n    // Verify there ARE lost docs before delta pass\n    let lost_before = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    assert!(\n        !lost_before.is_empty(),\n        \"Expected some lost docs before delta pass\"\n    );\n\n    // Delta pass repairs them\n    run_delta_pass(&mut coord, &mut cluster, mid, &old, &new, &shards);\n\n    assert_eq!(\n        coord.get_state(mid).unwrap().phase,\n        MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup\n    );\n    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Final: 0 loss\n    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    assert_eq!(\n        lost.len(),\n        0,\n        \"Lost {} docs with AE on + delta pass\",\n        lost.len()\n    );\n\n    let all = cluster.all_docs_for_shards(&shards);\n    assert_eq!(all.len(), 2100, \"Expected 2100 docs, got {}\", all.len());\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 2: AE on + delta skipped → measurable loss (AE would repair later)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_skip_delta_with_ae() {\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: new.clone()]);\n\n    for i in 0..500u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        cluster.put(&old, s, &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n    }\n\n    let mid =  }\n\n    // Register writes so drain can complete\n    for w in &writes {\n        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, &old, &new));\n    }\n\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n    let ComputingAssignments → DualWriteMigrating\n    for i in 0..50u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"b1-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            false,\n        );\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Burst 2: during DualWriteMigrating, some fail on new\n    for i in 0..100u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let new_fails = i % 25 == 0;\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"b2-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Burst 3: just before each shard_migration_complete\n    for &s in &shards {\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"b3-{s:?}\"),\n            false,\n            false,\n        );\n        all_writes.push(w);\n        coord.shard_migration_complete(mid, s, 300).unwrap();\n    }\n\n    // Burst 4: CutoverBegin → begin_cutover\n    for i in 0..50u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"b4-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            false,\n        );\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Register all completed writes for drain\n    for w in &all_writes {\n        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, &old, &new));\n    }\n\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Burst 5: during CutoverDraining — these go to old only\n    // In production, the delta pass catches these. We register them as\n    // failed on new so drain completes.\n    for i in 0..50u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let doc_id = format!(\"b5-{i}\");\n        cluster.put(&old, s, &doc_id);\n        // Not on new — will be caught by delta pass\n        let w = RecordedWrite {\n            doc_id: doc_id.clone(),\n            shard: s,\n            succeeded_on_old: true,\n            succeeded_on_new: false,\n        };\n        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(&w, &old, &new));\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n\n    run_delta_pass(&mut coord, &mut cluster, mid, &old, &new, &shards);\n\n    assert_eq!(\n        coord.get_state(mid).unwrap().phase,\n        MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup\n    );\n    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n\n    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    assert_eq!(lost.len(), 0, \"Boundary burst lost {} docs\", lost.len());\n\n    let all = cluster.all_docs_for_shards(&shards);\n    // 500 pre + 50 b1 + 100 b2 + 2 b3 + 50 b4 + 50 b5 = 752\n    assert!(all.len() >= 750, \"Expected >= 750 docs, got {}\", all.len());\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 6: high volume — 100K writes, measure loss rate with AE + delta\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_high_volume() {\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n        skip_delta_pass: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n\n    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n    let shards = vec![shard(0)];\n    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s, old.clone())).collect();\n\n    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(), new.clone()]);\n\n    const TOTAL: u64 = 100_000;\n\n    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n        cluster.put(&old, shards[0], &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n    }\n\n    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // 1% failure on new, but we don't register as in-flight for perf.\n    // We register a representative sample to drive delta pass.\n    for i in 0..TOTAL {\n        let doc_id = format!(\"w-{i}\");\n        let new_fails = i % 100 == 0;\n        dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            shards[0],\n            &doc_id,\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n    }\n\n    coord\n        .shard_migration_complete(mid, shards[0], 1000)\n        .unwrap();\n\n    // Boundary writes\n    for i in 0..100u64 {\n        dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            shards[0],\n            &format!(\"bnd-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            false,\n        );\n    }\n\n    // Register one failed write to force delta pass\n    coord.register_in_flight(InFlightWrite {\n        doc_id: \"w-0\".into(),\n        shard: shards[0],\n        target_nodes: vec![old.clone(), new.clone()],\n        completed_nodes: HashSet::from([old.clone()]),\n        failed_nodes: HashMap::from([(new.clone(), \"simulated failure\".into())]),\n        submitted_at: Instant::now(),\n    });\n\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n\n    // Delta pass\n    let lost: Vec<String> = cluster\n        .data\n        .get(&old)\n        .and_then(|m| m.get(&shards[0]))\n        .map(|docs| {\n            docs.iter()\n                .filter(|d| {\n                    !cluster\n                        .data\n                        .get(&new)\n                        .and_then(|m| m.get(&shards[0]))\n                        .is_some_and(|nd| nd.contains(*d))\n                })\n                .cloned()\n                .collect()\n        })\n        .unwrap_or_default();\n\n    let delta_count = lost.len();\n    for doc_id in &lost {\n        cluster.put(&new, shards[0], doc_id);\n    }\n    coord\n        .shard_delta_complete(mid, shards[0], delta_count as u64)\n        .unwrap();\n    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n\n    let lost_after = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    assert_eq!(\n        lost_after.len(),\n        0,\n        \"High-volume: lost {}/{} writes ({}%)\",\n        lost_after.len(),\n        TOTAL,\n        (lost_after.len() as f64 / TOTAL as f64) * 100.0\n    );\n\n    let all = cluster.all_docs_for_shards(&shards);\n    let expected = 1000 + TOTAL as usize + 100;\n    assert_eq!(all.len(), expected);\n\n    eprintln!(\n        \"\\n=== High Volume ({}K writes) ===\\n\\\n         Writes failed on new during dual-write: {}\\n\\\n         Caught by delta pass: {}\\n\\\n         Lost after delta pass: 0\\n\\\n         Loss rate: 0/{TOTAL} (0.000%)\\n\",\n        TOTAL / 1000,\n        TOTAL / 100,\n        delta_count,\n    );\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 7: AE off + delta on, 50K writes — confirm 0 loss rate\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_loss_rate_no_ae_delta() {\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n        skip_delta_pass: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n\n    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n    let shards = vec![shard(0), shard(1)];\n    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s, old.clone())).collect();\n\n    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(), new.clone()]);\n\n    const TOTAL: u64 = 50_000;\n\n    for i in 0..500u64 {\n        cluster.put(&old, shards[i as usize % shards.len()], &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n    }\n\n    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n\n    let mut failure_count = 0u64;\n    for i in 0..TOTAL {\n        let doc_id = format!(\"w-{i}\");\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let new_fails = i % 100 == 0;\n        if new_fails {\n            failure_count += 1;\n        }\n        dual_write(&mut cluster, &old, &new, s, &doc_id, false, new_fails);\n    }\n\n    for &s in &shards {\n        coord.shard_migration_complete(mid, s, 300).unwrap();\n    }\n\n    // Register one failed write to force delta pass\n    coord.register_in_flight(InFlightWrite {\n        doc_id: \"w-0\".into(),\n        shard: shards[0],\n        target_nodes: vec![old.clone(), new.clone()],\n        completed_nodes: HashSet::from([old.clone()]),\n        failed_nodes: HashMap::from([(new.clone(), \"simulated failure\".into())]),\n        submitted_at: Instant::now(),\n    });\n\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n\n    run_delta_pass(&mut coord, &mut cluster, mid, &old, &new, &shards);\n    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n\n    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    assert_eq!(\n        lost.len(),\n        0,\n        \"Lost {} docs without AE but with delta pass\",\n        lost.len()\n    );\n\n    eprintln!(\n        \"\\n=== Loss Rate: AE OFF + Delta Pass ON ===\\n\\\n         Total writes: {TOTAL}\\n\\\n         Writes failed on new during dual-write: {failure_count}\\n\\\n         Docs lost after delta pass: 0\\n\\\n         Loss rate: 0/{TOTAL} (0.000%)\\n\\\n         Conclusion: Delta pass alone provides 0-loss cutover.\\n\"\n    );\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 8: validation gates block unsafe configuration\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_validation_gates() {\n    use miroir_core::anti_entropy::{validate_migration_safety, AntiEntropyConfig};\n\n    // Gate 1: MigrationCoordinator refuses unsafe config\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n        skip_delta_pass: true,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n    assert!(coord.validate_safety().is_err());\n\n    // Gate 2: Cross-module anti_entropy validation\n    let ae = AntiEntropyConfig {\n        enabled: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let mc = MigrationConfig {\n        skip_delta_pass: true,\n        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    assert!(validate_migration_safety(&ae, &mc).is_err());\n\n    // Gate 3: Warning when AE disabled\n    use miroir_core::anti_entropy::migration_warning_if_ae_disabled;\n    assert!(migration_warning_if_ae_disabled(false).is_some());\n    assert!(migration_warning_if_ae_disabled(true).is_none());\n\n    // Safe configs should pass\n    let safe_config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n        skip_delta_pass: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let safe_coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(safe_config);\n    assert!(safe_coord.validate_safety().is_ok());\n\n    let safe_ae = AntiEntropyConfig {\n        enabled: true,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let safe_mc = MigrationConfig {\n        skip_delta_pass: true,\n        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    assert!(validate_migration_safety(&safe_ae, &safe_mc).is_ok());\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 9: tight-loop boundary — writes at exact cutover transition instant\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//\n// Simulates docs arriving at the instant of `active` transition (step 7 in\n// plan §2 \"Adding a node\"). The dangerous window is between CutoverBegin and\n// CutoverCleanup. Writes that succeed on OLD but fail on NEW during this\n// window MUST be caught by the delta pass.\n//\n// This variant drives writes at every single state transition boundary with\n// deterministic 5% failure injection on the new node.\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_tight_loop_boundary() {\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n        skip_delta_pass: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n\n    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n    let shards = vec![shard(0), shard(1), shard(2)];\n    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s, old.clone())).collect();\n\n    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(), new.clone()]);\n\n    // Pre-populate 1000 docs\n    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        cluster.put(&old, s, &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n    }\n\n    let mut all_writes: Vec<RecordedWrite> = Vec::new();\n\n    // Phase: ComputingAssignments → begin_migration\n    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n\n    // Burst: writes BEFORE dual-write starts (should go to old only in prod,\n    // but we simulate them as dual-write for boundary testing)\n    for i in 0..200u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let new_fails = i % 20 == 0; // 5% failure\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"t0-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Transition: ComputingAssignments → DualWriteMigrating\n    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Burst: writes during active dual-write migration\n    for i in 0..500u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let new_fails = i % 20 == 0; // 5% failure\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"t1-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Transition: complete shard migrations one at a time, writing between each\n    for (idx, &s) in shards.iter().enumerate() {\n        // Writes between shard completions\n        for j in 0..50u64 {\n            let s2 = shards[j as usize % shards.len()];\n            let new_fails = j % 20 == 0;\n            let w = dual_write(\n                &mut cluster,\n                &old,\n                &new,\n                s2,\n                &format!(\"t2-{idx}-{j}\"),\n                false,\n                new_fails,\n            );\n            all_writes.push(w);\n        }\n        coord.shard_migration_complete(mid, s, 500).unwrap();\n    }\n\n    // Transition: CutoverBegin → begin_cutover\n    // Rapid-fire writes at the exact boundary\n    for i in 0..300u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let new_fails = i % 20 == 0;\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"t3-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Register all writes for drain tracking\n    for w in &all_writes {\n        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, &old, &new));\n    }\n\n    // Cutover: stop dual-write, drain in-flight\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Writes during draining — these go to old only\n    for i in 0..200u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let doc_id = format!(\"t4-{i}\");\n        cluster.put(&old, s, &doc_id);\n        let w = RecordedWrite {\n            doc_id: doc_id.clone(),\n            shard: s,\n            succeeded_on_old: true,\n            succeeded_on_new: false,\n        };\n        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(&w, &old, &new));\n        all_writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n\n    // Delta pass catches everything\n    run_delta_pass(&mut coord, &mut cluster, mid, &old, &new, &shards);\n\n    assert_eq!(\n        coord.get_state(mid).unwrap().phase,\n        MigrationPhase::CutoverCleanup\n    );\n    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Assert: 0 lost docs\n    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    assert_eq!(\n        lost.len(),\n        0,\n        \"Tight-loop boundary test lost {} docs\",\n        lost.len()\n    );\n\n    let all = cluster.all_docs_for_shards(&shards);\n    // 1000 pre + 200 t0 + 500 t1 + 150 t2 + 300 t3 + 200 t4 = 2350\n    assert!(\n        all.len() >= 2350,\n        \"Expected >= 2350 docs, got {}\",\n        all.len()\n    );\n\n    eprintln!(\n        \"\\n=== Tight-Loop Boundary ===\\n\\\n         Total writes at boundaries: {}\\n\\\n         Docs lost after delta pass: 0\\n\\\n         Loss rate: 0/{} (0.000%)\\n\",\n        all_writes.len(),\n        all_writes.len()\n    );\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 10: 1M write loss rate measurement — AE on + delta on\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//\n// Acceptance criterion: loss rate < 1 per 1M writes.\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_loss_rate_1m_ae_on() {\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n        skip_delta_pass: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n\n    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n    let shards = vec![shard(0)];\n    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s, old.clone())).collect();\n\n    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(), new.clone()]);\n\n    const TOTAL: u64 = 1_000_000;\n    const FAIL_RATE: u64 = 100; // 1% failure on new\n\n    // Pre-populate\n    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n        cluster.put(&old, shards[0], &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n    }\n\n    let mid = coord.begin_migration(new.clone(), 0, affected).unwrap();\n    coord.begin_dual_write(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // 1M writes with 1% deterministic failure on new\n    let mut failure_count = 0u64;\n    for i in 0..TOTAL {\n        let doc_id = format!(\"w-{i}\");\n        let new_fails = i % FAIL_RATE == 0;\n        if new_fails {\n            failure_count += 1;\n        }\n        dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            shards[0],\n            &doc_id,\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n    }\n\n    coord\n        .shard_migration_complete(mid, shards[0], 1000)\n        .unwrap();\n\n    // Boundary writes\n    for i in 0..500u64 {\n        dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            shards[0],\n            &format!(\"bnd-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            false,\n        );\n    }\n\n    // Register one known-failed write to force delta pass\n    coord.register_in_flight(InFlightWrite {\n        doc_id: \"w-0\".into(),\n        shard: shards[0],\n        target_nodes: vec![old.clone(), new.clone()],\n        completed_nodes: HashSet::from([old.clone()]),\n        failed_nodes: HashMap::from([(new.clone(), \"simulated failure\".into())]),\n        submitted_at: Instant::now(),\n    });\n\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n    let phase = coord.complete_drain(mid).unwrap();\n    assert_eq!(phase, MigrationPhase::CutoverDeltaPass);\n\n    // Delta pass\n    let lost: Vec<String> = cluster\n        .data\n        .get(&old)\n        .and_then(|m| m.get(&shards[0]))\n        .map(|docs| {\n            docs.iter()\n                .filter(|d| {\n                    !cluster\n                        .data\n                        .get(&new)\n                        .and_then(|m| m.get(&shards[0]))\n                        .is_some_and(|nd| nd.contains(*d))\n                })\n                .cloned()\n                .collect()\n        })\n        .unwrap_or_default();\n\n    let delta_count = lost.len();\n    for doc_id in &lost {\n        cluster.put(&new, shards[0], doc_id);\n    }\n    coord\n        .shard_delta_complete(mid, shards[0], delta_count as u64)\n        .unwrap();\n    coord.complete_cleanup(mid).unwrap();\n\n    let lost_after = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    let loss_rate = lost_after.len() as f64 / TOTAL as f64;\n\n    assert_eq!(\n        lost_after.len(),\n        0,\n        \"1M write test: lost {}/{} writes ({:.6}%) — must be 0\",\n        lost_after.len(),\n        TOTAL,\n        loss_rate * 100.0\n    );\n\n    eprintln!(\n        \"\\n=== 1M Write Loss Rate: AE ON + Delta Pass ON ===\\n\\\n         Total writes: {TOTAL}\\n\\\n         Deterministic failures on new: {failure_count}\\n\\\n         Caught by delta pass: {delta_count}\\n\\\n         Lost after cutover: 0\\n\\\n         Loss rate: 0/{TOTAL} (0.000%)\\n\\\n         PASS: < 1 per 1M writes\\n\"\n    );\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 11: AE off + delta off → quantify loss rate (NOT started, refused)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//\n// This configuration is refused by the MigrationCoordinator. We bypass the\n// coordinator to measure what WOULD happen — the loss rate justifies the\n// hard refusal policy.\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_loss_rate_no_ae_no_delta() {\n    // This config is unsafe — the coordinator would refuse it.\n    // We construct a bare cluster to measure what would happen.\n    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n    let shards = vec![shard(0)];\n    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(), new.clone()]);\n\n    const TOTAL: u64 = 100_000;\n    const FAIL_RATE: u64 = 50; // 2% failure on new\n\n    // Pre-populate\n    for i in 0..1000u64 {\n        cluster.put(&old, shards[0], &format!(\"pre-{i}\"));\n    }\n\n    // Simulate dual-write without delta pass or AE\n    let mut lost_count = 0u64;\n    for i in 0..TOTAL {\n        let doc_id = format!(\"w-{i}\");\n        let new_fails = i % FAIL_RATE == 0;\n        dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            shards[0],\n            &doc_id,\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n        if new_fails {\n            lost_count += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Boundary writes (all succeed)\n    for i in 0..500u64 {\n        dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            shards[0],\n            &format!(\"bnd-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            false,\n        );\n    }\n\n    // Measure what's on old but not on new\n    let lost = cluster.lost_docs(&old, &new, &shards);\n    let loss_rate = lost.len() as f64 / TOTAL as f64;\n\n    // Pre-existing docs (1000) are also lost since we skipped background\n    // migration. Focus on dual-write losses.\n    assert!(\n        lost_count > 0,\n        \"Expected measurable loss without delta pass\"\n    );\n    assert_eq!(\n        lost_count,\n        lost.len() as u64 - 1000, // subtract pre-existing\n        \"Dual-write losses don't match expected count\"\n    );\n\n    eprintln!(\n        \"\\n=== Loss Rate: AE OFF + Delta OFF (hypothetical) ===\\n\\\n         Total writes: {TOTAL}\\n\\\n         Dual-write failures (old ok, new failed): {lost_count}\\n\\\n         Total docs missing on new (incl. pre-existing): {}\\n\\\n         Dual-write loss rate: {}/{TOTAL} ({:.4}%)\\n\\\n         Decision: MigrationCoordinator REFUSES this configuration.\\n\\\n         Justification: {:.4}% loss rate is unacceptable.\\n\",\n        lost.len(),\n        lost_count,\n        loss_rate * 100.0,\n        loss_rate * 100.0\n    );\n\n    // Verify the coordinator does refuse\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: false,\n        skip_delta_pass: true,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n    assert!(\n        coord.validate_safety().is_err(),\n        \"Coordinator must refuse unsafe config\"\n    );\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 12: concurrent writes during entire migration lifecycle\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n//\n// Simulates a realistic workload: writes arriving continuously through the\n// entire migration lifecycle, including at the exact CutoverActivate and\n// CutoverCleanup transitions.\n\n#[test]\nfn cutover_chaos_concurrent_migration_writes() {\n    let config = MigrationConfig {\n        anti_entropy_enabled: true,\n        skip_delta_pass: false,\n        ..Default::default()\n    };\n    let mut coord = MigrationCoordinator::new(config);\n\n    let old = node(\"old-0\");\n    let new = node(\"new-3\");\n    let shards = vec![shard(0), shard(1)];\n    let affected: HashMap<ShardId, NodeId> = shards.iter().map(|&s| (s, old.clone())).collect();\n\n    let mut cluster = SimCluster::new(&[old.clone(),            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"cw-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n        writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Complete shard s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let new_fails = i % 50 == 0;\n        let w = dual_write(\n            &mut cluster,\n            &old,\n            &new,\n            s,\n            &format!(\"cb-{i}\"),\n            false,\n            new_fails,\n        );\n        writes.push(w);\n    }\n\n    // Register for drain\n    for w in &writes {\n        coord.register_in_flight(make_in_flight(w, &old, &new));\n    }\n\n    coord.begin_cutover(mid).unwrap();\n\n    // Writes during draining (old only)\n    for i in 0..300u64 {\n        let s = shards[i as usize % shards.len()];\n        let doc_id = format!(\"cd-{i}\");\n        cluster.put(&old, s, &doc_id);\n        let w = RecordedWrite {\n            doc_id: doc_id.clone(),\n ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Test 13: 3-node cluster cutover — matches task design exactly\n// {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"call_50c3ed1c0bb24525b3c48ab4","type":"tool_result","content":"1\t//! Shard migration cutover state machine.\n2\t//!\n3\t//! Implements the node-addition migration flow from plan §4 with explicit state\n4\t//! transitions and a race-window-safe cutover sequence.\n5\t//!\n6\t//! ## Race window analysis (plan §15 OP#1)\n7\t//!\n8\t//! The dangerous window is between \"mark node active\" (routing changes to new-node-only)\n9\t//! and \"delete migrated shard from old node.\" A document written during dual-write that\n10\t//! succeeded on OLD but failed on NEW — and arrived after the last migration page —\n11\t//! would be deleted from OLD without ever reaching NEW.\n12\t//!\n13\t//! ## Solution: quiesce-then-verify cutover\n14\t//!\n15\t//! Instead of the naïve sequence (mark active → stop dual-write → delete old), we use:\n16\t//!\n17\t//! 1. Stop dual-write (no new writes go to either node for affected shards)\n18\t//! 2. Drain: wait for all in-flight writes to both OLD and NEW to complete\n19\t//! 3. Delta migration: re-read affected shards from OLD (catches anything written since\n20\t//!    the last migration page) and write deltas to NEW\n21\t//! 4. Mark node active (routing switches to NEW-only)\n22\t//! 5. Delete migrated shard from OLD\n23\t//!\n24\t//! Step 3 is the key: it closes the race window by ensuring NEW has a complete picture\n25\t//! before we commit the routing change. The cost is one extra pagination pass over each\n26\t//! migrated shard — bounded by the number of docs written during the migration window.\n27\t\n28\tuse std::collections::{HashMap, HashSet};\n29\tuse std::fmt;\n30\tuse std::time::{Duration, Instant};\n31\t\n32\tuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n33\t\n34\t/// Unique identifier for a shard migration operation.\n35\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n36\tpub struct MigrationId(pub u64);\n37\t\n38\timpl fmt::Display for MigrationId {\n39\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n40\t        write!(f, \"{}\", self.0)\n41\t    }\n42\t}\n43\t\n44\t/// Identifier for a physical node in the cluster.\n45\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n46\tpub struct NodeId(pub String);\n47\t\n48\t// Type alias for external use (rebalancer, etc.)\n49\tpub type MigrationNodeId = NodeId;\n50\t\n51\timpl fmt::Display for NodeId {\n52\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n53\t        write!(f, \"{}\", self.0)\n54\t    }\n55\t}\n56\t\n57\t/// Identifier for a logical shard.\n58\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n59\tpub struct ShardId(pub u32);\n60\t\n61\timpl fmt::Display for ShardId {\n62\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n63\t        write!(f, \"s{}\", self.0)\n64\t    }\n65\t}\n66\t\n67\t/// Per-shard migration state within a node-addition migration.\n68\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n69\tpub enum ShardMigrationState {\n70\t    /// Waiting for background migration to begin.\n71\t    Pending,\n72\t    /// Background pagination is reading docs from source and writing to target.\n73\t    Migrating {\n74\t        docs_copied: u64,\n75\t        pages_remaining: u32,\n76\t    },\n77\t    /// Background migration complete, awaiting cutover.\n78\t    MigrationComplete { docs_copied: u64 },\n79\t    /// Dual-write stopped, in-flight writes draining.\n80\t    Draining {\n81\t        in_flight_count: u32,\n82\t        docs_copied: u64,\n83\t    },\n84\t    /// Delta pass: re-reading source to catch stragglers written during migration.\n85\t    DeltaPass {\n86\t        docs_copied: u64,\n87\t        delta_docs_copied: u64,\n88\t    },\n89\t    /// Node is active for this shard; old replica data deleted.\n90\t    Active,\n91\t    /// Migration failed at this phase.\n92\t    Failed { phase: String, reason: String },\n93\t}\n94\t\n95\timpl fmt::Display for ShardMigrationState {\n96\t    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {\n97\t        match self {\n98\t            Self::Pending => write!(f, \"pending\"),\n99\t            Self::Migrating {\n100\t                docs_copied,\n101\t                pages_remaining,\n102\t            } => {\n103\t                write!(\n104\t                    f,\n105\t                    \"migrating({docs_copied} copied, {pages_remaining} pages left)\"\n106\t                )\n107\t            }\n108\t            Self::MigrationComplete { docs_copied } => {\n109\t                write!(f, \"migration_complete({docs_copied} copied)\")\n110\t            }\n111\t            Self::Draining {\n112\t                in_flight_count,\n113\t                docs_copied,\n114\t            } => {\n115\t                write!(\n116\t                    f,\n117\t                    \"draining({in_flight_count} in-flight, {docs_copied} copied)\"\n118\t                )\n119\t            }\n120\t            Self::DeltaPass {\n121\t                docs_copied,\n122\t                delta_docs_copied,\n123\t            } => {\n124\t                write!(f, \"delta_pass({docs_copied} + {delta_docs_copied} copied)\")\n125\t            }\n126\t            Self::Active => write!(f, \"active\"),\n127\t            Self::Failed { phase, reason } => write!(f, \"failed({phase}: {reason})\"),\n128\t        }\n129\t    }\n130\t}\n131\t\n132\t/// Overall migration phase for a node addition.\n133\t#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)]\n134\tpub enum MigrationPhase {\n135\t    /// Computing which shards move to the new node.\n136\t    ComputingAssignments,\n137\t    /// Dual-write active; background
